hagia_sophia = {
	start = 151
	date = 537.01.01
	time = { months = 0	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 2
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = apostolic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = syriac
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = nestorian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
		is_capital = yes
	}

	on_built = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = hagia_sophia_now_mosque
			}
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		}
		else = {
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
		}
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = apostolic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = syriac
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = nestorian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
		is_capital = yes
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = apostolic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = syriac
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = nestorian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
		is_capital = yes
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 0.25
			tolerance_heretic = 0.25
			move_capital_cost_modifier = 0.25
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 0.5
			tolerance_heretic = 0.5
			monthly_piety = 0.001
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.002
			papal_influence = 0.5
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
			move_capital_cost_modifier = 0.5
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 1
			tolerance_heretic = 1
			monthly_piety = 0.002
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.005
			papal_influence = 1
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
			move_capital_cost_modifier = 1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

stonehenge = {
	start = 10357

	can_be_moved = yes
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 2
	starting_tier = 0

	build_trigger = {

		#AND = {

		#		has_owner_culture = yes
		#		has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		#	}
		#}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = stonehenge
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = stonehenge

		OR = {
			AND = {

				culture = english

					has_owner_culture = yes

			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {

			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes

	}

		}
	}

		}
		area_modifier = {
		}

			tolerance_heretic = 0.5
			tolerance_heathen = 0.5
		}


		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_heretic = 0.5
			tolerance_heathen = 0.5
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_heretic = 1
			tolerance_heathen = 1
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.25
			global_missionary_strength = 0.01
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

buddha_statues = {
	start = 9455
	date = 570.01.01
	time = { months = 0 }
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = yes
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = buddha_small
		show_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_small
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_missionary_strength = 0.01
			local_missionary_maintenance_cost = -0.05
		}
		region_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -0.5
		}
		country_modifiers = {

	tier_2 = {

parthenon = {
	start = 146
	date = -432.01.01
	time = {
		months = 0
	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 6
	starting_tier = 0
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine_g
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
				has_global_flag = parthenon_now_mosque
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = parthenon_now_mosque
			}
			show_ambient_object = parthenon_minaret
		}
		else = {
			show_ambient_object = parthenon
		}
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = parthenon_minaret
		hide_ambient_object = parthenon
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine_g
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
				has_global_flag = parthenon_now_mosque
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine_g
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
				has_global_flag = parthenon_now_mosque
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -1
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			advisor_cost = -0.05
			move_capital_cost_modifier = 0.25
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -2
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			advisor_cost = -0.1
			move_capital_cost_modifier = 0.5
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -3
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			advisor_cost = -0.15
			advisor_pool = 1
			move_capital_cost_modifier = 1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

	start = 609

	time = { months = 0 }
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = dharmic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = angkor_wat
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = angkor_wat
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = dharmic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}

				has_owner_religion = yes

			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = dharmic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}

			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = borobudur_temple
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = borobudur_temple
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = malay
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = malay
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {

		on_upgraded = {

	}

	tier_1 = {

		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.15
		}

		}
		region_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -1
			#local_religious_unity_contribution = 0.03
		}

		}

	tier_2 = {

		}

		}

		}

		}

leshan_giant_buddha = {
	start = 4212 #Jiading
	date = 803.01.22
	time = { months = 0	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = buddha_small
		show_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_small
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {

			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {

	}

		}

		}

			local_missionary_strength = 0.01
			local_missionary_maintenance_cost = -0.05
		}

		}

	tier_2 = {

		}

	start = 94


	date = 963.1.1 #earlier, but this is when it sorta became important


	time = {
		months = 0
	}


	build_cost = 0


	can_be_moved = no


	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10


	starting_tier = 1


	type = monument


	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				culture_group = french
				OR = {
						has_owner_culture = yes
						has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = germanic
			OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			}

		}

			local_prosperity_growth = 0.5
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { trade_goods = chinaware }
				}
				change_trade_goods = chinaware
			}
			else = { add_base_production = 1 }
		}
	}

			local_prosperity_growth = 1

		}
		on_upgraded = {

				limit = {
					NOT = { trade_goods = chinaware }
				}
				change_trade_goods = chinaware
			}
			else = { add_base_production = 1 }
		}
	}

palace_of_the_popes = {
	start = 202 #Avignon
	date = 1335.10.07
	time = { months = 0	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		province_is_or_accepts_religion_group = {
			religion_group = christian
		}
	}

	on_built = {
	}

	on_destroyed = {
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		province_is_or_accepts_religion_group = {
			religion_group = christian
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		province_is_or_accepts_religion_group = {
			religion_group = christian
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_governing_cost = -0.15
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			church_privilege_slots = 1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven" }
				owner = { add_splendor = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					202 = { has_cardinal = no }
					owner = { religion = catholic }
				}
				202 = { add_cardinal = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_governing_cost = -0.25
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			church_privilege_slots = 1
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
			papal_influence = 1
			church_power_modifier = 0.25
			monthly_fervor_increase = 0.3
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven" }
				owner = {
					add_power_projection = {
						type = mission_rewards_power_projection
						amount = 25
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					202 = { has_cardinal = no }
					owner = { religion = catholic }
				}
				202 = { add_cardinal = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_governing_cost = -0.33
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			church_privilege_slots = 1
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.15
			papal_influence = 2
			church_power_modifier = 0.33
			monthly_fervor_increase = 0.5
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven" }
				owner = {
					add_power_projection = {
						type = mission_rewards_power_projection
						amount = 50
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					202 = { has_cardinal = no }

xian_walls = {
	start = 700
	date = 1380.01.01
	time = { months = 0 }
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 7
	starting_tier = 2
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	on_built = {
	}

	on_destroyed = {
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	}

	tier_0 = {

		}

		}
		country_modifiers = {
			#war_taxes_cost_modifier = -0.5

			move_capital_cost_modifier = 0.25
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {

			months = 240
		}

		}

			local_manpower_modifier = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}
		area_modifier = {
			regiment_recruit_speed = -0.25
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			#war_taxes_cost_modifier = -0.5
			#prestige_from_land = 1
			#general_cost = -0.1
			move_capital_cost_modifier = 0.5
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {

		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_manpower_modifier = 0.66
			local_defensiveness = 0.35
		}
